Question: 3
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: Subtract 153 from 200.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The final answer is 47. To arrive at this answer, you subtract 153 from 200. This is done by subtracting the tens digit, 0, from 2, which gives you 2. Then, you subtract the ones digit, 3, from 1, which gives you -2. Since you cannot subtract a negative number from a positive number, you must borrow from the tens digit. You then subtract 1 from 2, which gives you 1. You then subtract 3 from 10, which gives you 7. Therefore, 200 - 153 = 47.

You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: What is the average of 2, 4, 6, 8?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The average of 2, 4, 6, 8 is 5.5. To find the average, you add the numbers together and divide by the number of numbers. In this case, you add 2 + 4 + 6 + 8 = 20. Then, you divide 20 by 4, which is the number of numbers. So, the average is 20/4 = 5.5.

Question: What is the area of a circle with a radius of 5?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The final answer is 78.54. To find the area of a circle with a radius of 5, you use the formula A = πr^2, where A is the area, π is pi (approximately 3.14), and r is the radius. Substituting the values, you get A = 3.14 x 5^2, which equals 78.54.

Question: What is the volume of a cylinder with a radius of 2 and a height of 6?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The final answer is 44.66. To find the volume of a cylinder with a radius of 2 and a height of 6, you use the formula V = πr^2h, where V is the volume, π is pi (approximately 3.14), r is the radius, and h is the height. Substituting the values, you get V = 3.14 x 2^2 x 6, which equals 44.66.

Question: What is the area of a square with a side length of 5?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The final answer is 25. To find the area of a square with a side length of 5, you use the formula A = s^2, where A is the area, s is the side length. Substituting the values, you get A = 5^2, which equals 25.

Question: What is the volume of a rectangular prism with a length of 6, a width of 4, and a height of 3?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The final answer is 108. To find the volume of a rectangular prism with a length of 6, a width of 4, and a height of 3, you use the formula V = lwh, where V is the volume, l is the length, w is the width, and h is the height. Substituting the values, you get V = 6 x 4 x 3, which equals 108.

Question: What is the area of a triangle with a base of 10 and a height of 5?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The final answer is 50. To find the area of a triangle with a base of 10 and a height of 5, you use the formula A = (1/2)bh, where A is the area, b is the base, and h is the height. Substituting the values, you get A = (1/2) x 10 x 5, which equals 25. However, since the area must be positive, you multiply the answer by 2, which gives you 50.

Question: What is the volume of a cone with a radius of 3 and a height of 4?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The final answer is 18. To find the volume of a cone with a radius of 3 and a height of 4, you use the formula V = (1/3)πr^2h, where V is the volume, π is pi (approximately 3.14), r is the radius, and h is the height. Substituting the values, you get V = (1/3) x 3.14 x 3^2 x 4, which equals 18.

Question: Solve: 3x + 7 = 22

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: To solve the equation 3x + 7 = 22, we need to isolate the variable x. We can do this by subtracting 7 from both sides of the equation. This gives us 3x = 22 - 7, which simplifies to 3x = 15. To solve for x, we need to divide both sides of the equation by 3. This gives us x = 15/3, which simplifies to x = 5. Therefore, the solution to the equation 3x + 7 = 22 is x = 5.

Question: What is the area of a circle with radius 10 cm?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The area of a circle is calculated as follows:

Area = π x (Radius)²
Area = π x (10 cm)²
Area = π x 100 cm²
Area = 3.14 x 100 cm²
Area = 314 cm²



,

Question: What is the volume of a cylinder with radius 2 cm and height 4 cm?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The volume of a cylinder is calculated as follows:

Volume = π x (Radius)² x Height
Volume = π x (2 cm)² x 4 cm
Volume = π x 4 cm² x 4 cm
Volume = π x 16 cm³
Volume = 3.14 x 16 cm³
Volume = 50.24 cm³



,

Question: 26
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: A pie chart shows 40% red, 30% blue, 30% green. If there are 200 people, how many prefer blue?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: There are 60 people who prefer blue.

Explanation: To find the number of people who prefer blue, we need to multiply the percentage of blue by the total number of people. We know that 40% of the people prefer red, 30% prefer blue, and 30% prefer green. We can add these percentages together to find the total percentage of people who prefer blue. 40% + 30% + 30% = 100%. We know that there are 200 people in total, so we can divide the percentage of blue by the total number of people to find the number of people who prefer blue. 30% ÷ 100% = 0.3. We can multiply this number by the total number of people to find the number of people who prefer blue. 0.3 x 200 = 60.

Answer: x = 2 or x = 3

Factor the quadratic equation:

(x - 2)(x - 3) = 0

Set each factor equal to zero:

x - 2 = 0
x - 3 = 0

Solve for x:

x = 2
x = 3

Question: 35
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: A ladder leans against a wall forming a right triangle. If base = 6m, height = 8m, find length of ladder.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The ladder is leaning against a wall forming a right triangle. The base of the triangle is 6m and the height is 8m. We can use the Pythagorean theorem to find the length of the ladder. The Pythagorean theorem states that the square of the hypotenuse (the side opposite the right angle) is equal to the sum of the squares of the other two sides. In this case, the hypotenuse is the ladder and the other two sides are the base and the height.

Using the Pythagorean theorem, we can write the equation:

c^2 = a^2 + b^2

where c is the length of the hypotenuse, a is the length of the base, and b is the length of the height.

Substituting the given values, we get:

c^2 = 6^2 + 8^2

c^2 = 36 + 64

c^2 = 100

Taking the square root of both sides, we get:

c = √100

c = 10

Therefore, the length of the ladder is 10m.

Question: 36
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: Compound interest on ₹5000 at 10% for 2 years.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The final amount is ₹6500. Compound interest is calculated by adding the interest to the principal amount and then adding the interest to the new principal amount. The formula is A = P(1 + r/n)^(nt), where A is the final amount, P is the principal amount, r is the interest rate, n is the number of times the interest is compounded per year, and t is the number of years. In this case, A = ₹5000(1 + 0.10/1)^(1*2) = ₹6500.

Question: 37
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: A train travels at 90 km/h. It takes 1.5 hours more than another train at 120 km/h. Find the distance.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The train at 90 km/h travels at a speed of 90 km/h × 1.5 = 135 km/h.

The train at 120 km/h travels at a speed of 120 km/h.

The difference in speed between the two trains is 120 km/h − 90 km/h = 30 km/h.

The time difference between the two trains is 1.5 hours.

The time difference is equal to the difference in speed, so the distance between the two trains is 135 km/h × 1.5 hours = 202.5 km.

Question: 38
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: A bag contains 5 red, 3 blue, 2 green balls. Two drawn without replacement. Find probability both are red.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The probability of drawing two red balls is 1/10.

Explanation: There are a total of 10 balls in the bag. The probability of drawing a red ball on the first draw is 5/10. Since the ball is not replaced, there are now 4 red balls left in the bag. The probability of drawing a red ball on the second draw is 4/9. The probability of both events happening is the product of the two probabilities, so the probability of drawing two red balls is (5/10) * (4/9) = 1/10.

The probability of both events happening is the product of the two probabilities, so the probability of drawing two red balls is (3/6) * (2/5) = 1/5.

Question: 39
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: What is the standard deviation of: 2, 4, 4, 4, 5, 5, 7, 9?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The standard deviation of the given data set is 1.21. This is calculated by taking the square root of the variance, which is 2.25.

Explanation: The variance is calculated by subtracting the mean from each data point, squaring the result, and then averaging the squared differences. In this case, the mean is 5, so the squared differences are (2-5)^2, (4-5)^2, (4-5)^2, (4-5)^2, (5-5)^2, (5-5)^2, (7-5)^2, and (9-5)^2. These are 9, 1, 1, 1, 0, 0, 4, and 16. The average of these squared differences is 16+9+1+1+0+0+4+16/8 = 35/8 = 4.375. The variance is then 4.375 squared, or 19.1875. The standard deviation is the square root of the variance, or sqrt(19.1875) = 4.24. However, since the data set is already ordered, we can use the formula for the standard deviation of an ordered data set, which is the square root of the variance divided by the number of data points minus one. In this case, the number of data points is 8, so the standard deviation is sqrt(19.1875)/7 = 1.21.

Subtract 2 from both sides: -7 > x










The solution is x < -7.










Explanation: We subtracted 2x from both sides to isolate x on one side of the inequality. We then subtracted 2 from both sides to isolate x further. The final solution is x < -7.

Question: 44
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: A cone has height 12 cm, base radius 5 cm. Find volume.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The volume of a cone is given by the formula V = (1/3)πr2h, where r is the radius of the base and h is the height of the cone. In this case, the radius is 5 cm and the height is 12 cm. Plugging these values into the formula, we get V = (1/3)π(5)2(12) = (1/3)π(25)(12) = (1/3)(314)(12) = 1256/3 = 418.67 cm3. Therefore, the volume of the cone is 418.67 cm3.



Question: A sphere has radius 10 cm. Find volume.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The volume of a sphere is given by the formula V = (4/3)πr3, where r is the radius of the sphere. In this case, the radius is 10 cm. Plugging this value into the formula, we get V = (4/3)π(10)3 = (4/3)π(100) = (4/3)(3.14)(100) = 418.67 cm3. Therefore, the volume of the sphere is 418.67 cm3.



Question: A cylinder has height 12 cm, base radius 5 cm. Find volume.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The volume of a cylinder is given by the formula V = πr2h, where r is the radius of the base and h is the height of the cylinder. In this case, the radius is 5 cm and the height is 12 cm. Plugging these values into the formula, we get V = π(5)2(12) = π(25)(12) = 314π cm3. Therefore, the volume of the cylinder is 314π cm3.



Question: A cylinder has height 12 cm, base radius 5 cm. Find surface area.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The surface area of a cylinder is given by the formula A = 2πrh + 2πr2, where r is the radius of the base and h is the height of the cylinder. In this case, the radius is 5 cm and the height is 12 cm. Plugging these values into the formula, we get A = 2π(5)(12) + 2π(5)2 = 2π(60) + 2π(25) = 120π + 50π = 170π cm2. Therefore, the surface area of the cylinder is 170π cm2.



Question: A cylinder has height 12 cm, base radius 5 cm. Find the surface area.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The surface area of a cylinder is given by the formula A = 2πrh + 2πr2, where r is the radius of the base and h is the height of the cylinder. In this case, the radius is 5 cm and the height is 12 cm. Plugging these values into the formula, we get A = 2π(5)(12) + 2π(5)2 = 120π + 50π = 170π cm2. Therefore, the surface area of the cylinder is 170π cm2.

Question: What's the angle between the hour and minute hand at 2:30?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The angle between the hour and minute hand at 2:30 is 30 degrees.

Explanation: At 2:30, the minute hand is pointing directly at the 6, and the hour hand is pointing at the 2. The angle between the hour and minute hand is the difference between the positions of the hands. The hour hand is 1/2 of the way between the 2 and the 3, so it is 1/2 of the way between the 180-degree mark and the 120-degree mark. The angle between the hour and minute hand is therefore 180 - 120 - 1/2 = 30 degrees.

Question: 48
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: A boat goes 30 km upstream in 3 hours and returns in 2. Find speed of boat and current.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: Let the speed of the boat be x km/h and the speed of the current be y km/h.

From the question, we know that the boat goes upstream for 3 hours and returns in 2 hours.

We can write the equation for the distance covered by the boat upstream as:

3x = 30

Solving for x, we get:

x = 10 km/h

We can write the equation for the distance covered by the boat downstream as:

2x = 30

Solving for x, we get:

x = 15 km/h

Now, we can write the equation for the speed of the boat as:

x + y = 15

Substituting the value of x, we get:

10 + y = 15

Solving for y, we get:

y = 5 km/h

Therefore, the speed of the boat is 15 km/h and the speed of the current is 5 km/h.

If base = 6m, height = 8m, find length of ladder.\n\nInstruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.\n\nAnswer: The ladder is leaning against a wall forming a right triangle. The base of the triangle is 6m and the height is 8m. We can use the Pythagorean theorem to find the length of the ladder. The Pythagorean theorem states that the square of the hypotenuse (the side opposite the right angle) is equal to the sum of the squares of the other two sides. In this case, the hypotenuse is the ladder and the other two sides are the base and the height.\n\nUsing the Pythagorean theorem, we can write the equation:\n\nc^2 = a^2 + b^2\n\nwhere c is the length of the hypotenuse, a is the length of the base, and b is the length of the height.\n\nSubstituting the given values, we get:\n\nc^2 = 6^2 + 8^2\n\nc^2 = 36 + 64\n\nc^2 = 100\n\nTaking the square root of both sides, we get:\n\nc = \u221a100\n\nc = 10\n\nTherefore, the length of the ladder is 10m.\n\nExplanation: The ladder is leaning against a wall forming a right triangle.     "You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.\n\nQuestion: A train travels at 90 km/h. It takes 1.5 hours more than another train at 120 km/h. Find the distance.\n\nInstruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.\n\nAnswer: The train at 90 km/h travels at a speed of 90 km/h \u00d7 1.5 = 135 km/h.\n\nThe train at 120 km/h travels at a speed of 120 km/h.\n\nThe difference in speed between the two trains is 120 km/h \u2212 90 km/h = 30 km/h.\n\nThe time difference between the two trains is 1.5 hours.\n\nThe time difference is equal to the difference in speed, so the distance between the two trains is 135 km/h \u00d7 1.5 hours = 202.5 km.\n\n\n\nQuestion: A train travels at 90 km/h.
